GP Trial Top 8 decklists
========================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on October 18, 2003 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20211024110319im_/https://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/themes/wiz_mtg/images/global/generic-avatar-150.png)
By Sideboard Staff











These are the sealed decklists from the GP trial held last night. In the top 8 Rochester draft, Brad Taulbee played Ryan Opalk, Ben Vrba played Troy Gould, Otto Schmidt played Kyle Saugier, and Luke Koleczek played Michael Dvorak. Unfortunately, there are no decklists available for the Rochester draft, as it was 4 AM before the draft concluded. The players apparently opted for sleep over decklists, but we certainly won't hold it against them.

The players who received byes are Brad Taulbee, Ben Vrba, Otto Schmidt, and Luke Koleczek. No doubt they've enjoyed their extra sleep, and are now ready to play in Round 4.






#### Brad Taulbee


##### 






![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)

[Sample Hand](#none)
